JAP_imperial_headquarters_landing_operations_decisions = {
	JAP_imperial_headquarters_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam = {
		icon = generic_naval
		cost = 0
		days_remove = 30
		priority = 85
		visible = {
			JAP_scripted_landing_enabled = yes
			591 = {
				state_is_fully_controlled_by_ROOT_subject_or_faction_member = yes
			}
			289 = {
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					state_is_fully_controlled_by_ROOT_subject_or_faction_member = yes
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			JAP_scripted_landing_naval_strength_available = yes
			JAP_scripted_landing_capacity_available = yes
			hidden_trigger = {
				289 = {
					JAP_scripted_landing_target_not_recently_landed = yes
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP_scripted_landing_raid_ready = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_imperial_headquarters_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_raid_tt
				591 = {
					save_event_target_as = JAP_scripted_landing_origin_state
				}
				289 = {
					save_event_target_as = JAP_scripted_landing_target_state
					hidden_effect = {
						JAP_void_landing_medium_with_big_damage = yes
						JAP_scripted_landing_mark_recent_landing_target = yes
					}
					JAP_scripted_landing_notify_target_controller_raid = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_raid_cooldown
					JAP_scripted_landing_reserve_medium_capacity = yes
					JAP_scripted_landing_reset_raid_counter = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_imperial_headquarters_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_plan_tt
				591 = {
					save_event_target_as = JAP_scripted_landing_origin_state
				}
				289 = {
					save_event_target_as = JAP_scripted_landing_target_state
					JAP_scripted_landing_notify_target_controller_plan = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_plan_pending
					JAP_scripted_landing_reserve_medium_capacity = yes
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_raid_cooldown
				}
				JAP_scripted_landing_release_medium_capacity = yes
				clr_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_raid_cooldown
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_plan_pending
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						591 = {
							state_is_fully_controlled_by_ROOT_subject_or_faction_member = yes
						}
						289 = {
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
							NOT = {
								state_is_fully_controlled_by_ROOT_subject_or_faction_member = yes
							}
							JAP_scripted_landing_target_not_recently_landed = yes
						}
					}
					289 = {
						JAP_void_landing_medium_with_small_damage = yes
						JAP_scripted_landing_mark_recent_landing_target = yes
					}
					JAP_scripted_landing_record_successful_regular_landing = yes
				}
				JAP_scripted_landing_release_medium_capacity = yes
				clr_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_plan_pending
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_plan_pending
			591 = {
				NOT = {
					state_is_fully_controlled_by_ROOT_subject_or_faction_member = yes
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_plan_pending
				}
				JAP_scripted_landing_release_medium_capacity = yes
				clr_country_flag = JAP_scripted_landing_hainan_to_siam_plan_pending
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 900
		}
	}
